function compound\+Write\+Get\+Complete\+Node (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{compound\+Write}{, }\item[{}]{path}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a node for a path if and only if the node is a "{}complete"{} overwrite at that path. This will not aggregate writes from deeper paths, but will return child nodes from a more shallow path.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hline
{\em path} & -\/ The path to get a complete write \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The node if complete at that path, or null otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{eventGeneratorGenerateEventsForChanges@{eventGeneratorGenerateEventsForChanges}!index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{eventGeneratorGenerateEventsForChanges()}{eventGeneratorGenerateEventsForChanges()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_aa06d6c99339cc31814c6866e5a47f48f} 
function event\+Generator\+Generate\+Events\+For\+Changes (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{event\+Generator}{, }\item[{}]{changes}{, }\item[{}]{event\+Cache}{, }\item[{}]{event\+Registrations}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Given a set of raw changes (no moved events and prev\+Name not specified yet), and a set of Event\+Registrations that should be notified of these changes, generate the actual events to be raised.

Notes\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item child\+\_\+moved events will be synthesized at this time for any child\+\_\+changed events that affect our index.
\item prev\+Name will be calculated based on the index ordering. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

References \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a20575f4946cf752f4af759655176ac6e}{change\+Child\+Moved()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_aa7f1ba8110aba9777982f140d8f9157e}{event\+Generator\+Generate\+Events\+For\+Type()}}.

Remove event \doxylink{database-compat_2dist_2index_8standalone_8js_a622460feeccdab6d8f307936fc6b36fb}{callback(s)}. Return cancel\+Events if a cancel\+Error is specified.

If query is the default query, we\textquotesingle{}ll check all views for the specified event\+Registration. If event\+Registration is null, we\textquotesingle{}ll remove all callbacks for the specified view(s).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event\+Registration} & -\/ If null, remove all callbacks. \\

{\em cancel\+Error} & -\/ If a cancel\+Error is provided, appropriate cancel events will be returned. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
removed queries and any cancel events 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a56f06a74c4c954b21a54ffa8b2bc2766}\index{index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}!syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_@{syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_}}
\index{syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_@{syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_}!index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_()}{syncTreeApplyOperationToSyncPoints\_()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a56f06a74c4c954b21a54ffa8b2bc2766} 
function sync\+Tree\+Apply\+Operation\+To\+Sync\+Points\+\_\+ (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{sync\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{operation}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxylink{class_a}{A} helper method that visits all descendant and ancestor Sync\+Points, applying the operation.

NOTES\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Descendant Sync\+Points will be visited first (since we raise events depth-\/first).
\item We call apply\+Operation() on each \doxylink{class_sync_point}{Sync\+Point} passing three things\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item \doxylink{class_a}{A} version of the \doxylink{class_operation}{Operation} that has been made relative to the \doxylink{class_sync_point}{Sync\+Point} location.
\item \doxylink{class_a}{A} Write\+Tree\+Ref of any writes we have cached at the \doxylink{class_sync_point}{Sync\+Point} location.
\item \doxylink{class_a}{A} snapshot \doxylink{class_node}{Node} with cached server data, if we have it.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\item We concatenate all of the events returned by each \doxylink{class_sync_point}{Sync\+Point} and return the result. 
\end{DoxyItemize}

\index{syncTreeCalcCompleteEventCache@{syncTreeCalcCompleteEventCache}!index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{syncTreeCalcCompleteEventCache()}{syncTreeCalcCompleteEventCache()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a8f74d44e0635cfa16a278f75dd5b43ed} 
function sync\+Tree\+Calc\+Complete\+Event\+Cache (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{sync\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{path}{, }\item[{}]{write\+Ids\+To\+Exclude}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a complete cache, if we have one, of the data at a particular path. If the location does not have a listener above it, we will get a false "{}null"{}. This shouldn\textquotesingle{}t be a problem because transactions will always have a listener above, and atomic operations would correctly show a jitter of $<$increment value$>$ -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} $<$incremented total$>$ as the write is applied locally and then acknowledged at the server.

Note\+: this method will {\itshape include} hidden writes from transaction with apply\+Locally set to false.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em path} & -\/ The path to the data we want \\
\hline
{\em write\+Ids\+To\+Exclude} & -\/ \doxylink{class_a}{A} specific set to be excluded \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{syncTreeRemoveEventRegistration()}{syncTreeRemoveEventRegistration()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_ae1d9310673b9a93a1006c5726434f36e} 
function sync\+Tree\+Remove\+Event\+Registration (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{sync\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{query}{, }\item[{}]{event\+Registration}{, }\item[{}]{cancel\+Error}{, }\item[{}]{skip\+Listener\+Dedup}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{database-compat_2dist_2index_8standalone_8js_a5df37b7f02e5cdc7d9412b7f872b8e01}{false}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Remove event \doxylink{database-compat_2dist_2index_8standalone_8js_a622460feeccdab6d8f307936fc6b36fb}{callback(s)}.

If query is the default query, we\textquotesingle{}ll check all queries for the specified event\+Registration. If event\+Registration is null, we\textquotesingle{}ll remove all callbacks for the specified query/queries.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em event\+Registration} & -\/ If null, all callbacks are removed. \\
\hline
{\em cancel\+Error} & -\/ If a cancel\+Error is provided, appropriate cancel events will be returned. \\
\hline
{\em skip\+Listener\+Dedup} & -\/ When performing a {\ttfamily \doxylink{response_8js_a10d7f5ef6343bd4575249458cf93dd3e}{get()}}, we don\textquotesingle{}t add any new listeners, so no deduping needs to take place. This flag allows toggling of that behavior \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Cancel events, if cancel\+Error was provided. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
We may have just removed one of many listeners and can short-\/circuit this whole process We may also not have removed a default listener, in which case all of the descendant listeners should already be properly set up.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeTreeCalcEventCacheAfterServerOverwrite()}{writeTreeCalcEventCacheAfterServerOverwrite()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a0af511a848b543e8b750577ca79511d8} 
function write\+Tree\+Calc\+Event\+Cache\+After\+Server\+Overwrite (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{write\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{tree\+Path}{, }\item[{}]{child\+Path}{, }\item[{}]{existing\+Event\+Snap}{, }\item[{}]{existing\+Server\+Snap}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Given that the underlying server data has updated, determine what, if anything, needs to be applied to the event cache.

Possibilities\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item No writes are shadowing. Events should be raised, the snap to be applied comes from the server data
\item Some write is completely shadowing. No events to be raised
\item Is partially shadowed. Events
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

Either existing\+Event\+Snap or existing\+Server\+Snap must exist 

References \mbox{\hyperlink{database-compat_2dist_2index_8standalone_8js_a445382df6f5596f104fa45c8dc67fa73}{assert}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a85826c9c6af411968b768e068b8cbdeb}{compound\+Write\+Apply()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a116780f9654565d18962386d8cec23ba}{compound\+Write\+Child\+Compound\+Write()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_ad93a1e7674b44729ff58a0de4b5cf3e7}{compound\+Write\+Has\+Complete\+Write()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_af0c9ad5ce40b17f9c4226ff68d6d5003}{compound\+Write\+Is\+Empty()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{cjs_2src_2bucket_8js_a1fdc7709faf62dce60620fb3f9d3453c}{path}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_ab9e284ca814159887379a486417d92ac}{path\+Child()}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeTreeRefCalcCompleteEventCache()}{writeTreeRefCalcCompleteEventCache()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a342f22c39b56a12f0a90b9d1491dd62e} 
function write\+Tree\+Ref\+Calc\+Complete\+Event\+Cache (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{write\+Tree\+Ref}{, }\item[{}]{complete\+Server\+Cache}{, }\item[{}]{write\+Ids\+To\+Exclude}{, }\item[{}]{include\+Hidden\+Writes}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If possible, returns a complete event cache, using the underlying server data if possible. In addition, can be used to get a cache that includes hidden writes, and excludes arbitrary writes. Note that customizing the returned node can lead to a more expensive calculation.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em write\+Ids\+To\+Exclude} & -\/ Optional writes to exclude. \\
\hline
{\em include\+Hidden\+Writes} & -\/ Defaults to false, whether or not to layer on writes with visible set to false \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeTreeRefCalcEventCacheAfterServerOverwrite()}{writeTreeRefCalcEventCacheAfterServerOverwrite()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a4f552e483713e3f24cc66885a7395f9a} 
function write\+Tree\+Ref\+Calc\+Event\+Cache\+After\+Server\+Overwrite (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{write\+Tree\+Ref}{, }\item[{}]{path}{, }\item[{}]{existing\+Event\+Snap}{, }\item[{}]{existing\+Server\+Snap}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Given that either the underlying server data has updated or the outstanding writes have updated, determine what, if anything, needs to be applied to the event cache.

Possibilities\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item No writes are shadowing. Events should be raised, the snap to be applied comes from the server data
\item Some write is completely shadowing. No events to be raised
\item Is partially shadowed. Events should be raised
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

Either existing\+Event\+Snap or existing\+Server\+Snap must exist, this is validated via an assert 

References \mbox{\hyperlink{cjs_2src_2bucket_8js_a1fdc7709faf62dce60620fb3f9d3453c}{path}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a0af511a848b543e8b750577ca79511d8}{write\+Tree\+Calc\+Event\+Cache\+After\+Server\+Overwrite()}}.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeTreeRemoveWrite()}{writeTreeRemoveWrite()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_ae3a9a5adb174d22e3fecc47a738655c1} 
function write\+Tree\+Remove\+Write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{write\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{write\+Id}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Remove a write (either an overwrite or merge) that has been successfully acknowledge by the server. Recalculates the tree if necessary. We return true if it may have been visible, meaning views need to reevaluate.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if the write may have been visible (meaning we\textquotesingle{}ll need to reevaluate / raise events as a result). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{writeTreeShadowingWrite()}{writeTreeShadowingWrite()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a13992415e37a1e1ce2d38210165bb932} 
function write\+Tree\+Shadowing\+Write (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{write\+Tree}{, }\item[{}]{path}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns a node if there is a complete overwrite for this path. More specifically, if there is a write at a higher path, this will return the child of that write relative to the write and this path. Returns null if there is no write at this path. 

References \mbox{\hyperlink{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_ad689312819edd45fd8af91f7f3fbd60a}{compound\+Write\+Get\+Complete\+Node()}}, and \mbox{\hyperlink{cjs_2src_2bucket_8js_a1fdc7709faf62dce60620fb3f9d3453c}{path}}.

\Hypertarget{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a2a554ba541fbbca6bcc6e80fcf9158f1}\index{index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}!buildChildSet@{buildChildSet}}
\index{buildChildSet@{buildChildSet}!index.node.esm.js@{index.node.esm.js}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{buildChildSet}{buildChildSet}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{database_2dist_2node-esm_2index_8node_8esm_8js_a2a554ba541fbbca6bcc6e80fcf9158f1} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{node__modules_2_0dgrpc_2grpc-js_2build_2src_2server_8js_a92b303b76a3f942ea819498907d5e83c}{const}} build\+Child\+Set}

Takes a list of child nodes and constructs a Sorted\+Set using the given comparison function

Uses the algorithm described in the paper linked here\+: \href{http://citeseerx.ist.psu.edu/viewdoc/summary?doi=10.1.1.46.1458}{\texttt{ http\+://citeseerx.\+ist.\+psu.\+edu/viewdoc/summary?doi=10.\+1.\+1.\+46.\+1458}}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em child\+List} & -\/ Unsorted list of children \\
\hline
{\em cmp} & -\/ The comparison method to be used \\
\hline
{\em key\+Fn} & -\/ An optional function to extract K from a node wrapper, if K\textquotesingle{}s type is not \doxylink{class_named_node}{Named\+Node} \\
\hline
{\em map\+Sort\+Fn} & -\/ An optional override for comparator used by the generated sorted map \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{throw}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{firestore__admin__v1__proto__api_8js_a08a4415e9d594ff960030b921d42b91e}{e}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}
Helper to run some code but catch any exceptions and re-\/throw them later. Useful for preventing user callbacks from breaking internal code.

Re-\/throwing the exception from a set\+Timeout is a little evil, but it\textquotesingle{}s very convenient (we don\textquotesingle{}t have to try to figure out when is a safe point to re-\/throw it), and the behavior seems reasonable\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If you aren\textquotesingle{}t pausing on exceptions, you get an error in the console with the correct stack trace.
\item If you\textquotesingle{}re pausing on all exceptions, the debugger will pause on your exception and then again when we rethrow it.
\item If you\textquotesingle{}re only pausing on uncaught exceptions, the debugger will only pause on us re-\/throwing it.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fn} & -\/ The code to guard. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

Same as set\+Timeout() except on Node.\+JS it will /not/ prevent the process from exiting.

It is removed with clear\+Timeout() as normal.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fn} & -\/ Function to run. \\
\hline
{\em time} & -\/ Milliseconds to wait before running. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The set\+Timeout() return value. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
